## Your Task

   116→HeaderValidator::HeaderValueValidationResult
   117→HeaderValidator::validateSchemeHeader(const HeaderString& value) {
   118→  // From RFC 3986, https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/html/rfc3986#section-3.1:
   119→  //
   120→  // scheme = ALPHA *( ALPHA / DIGIT / "+" / "-" / "." )
   121→  //
   122→  // Although schemes are case-insensitive, the canonical form is lowercase and documents that
   123→  // specify schemes must do so with lowercase letters. An implementation should accept uppercase
   124→  // letters as equivalent to lowercase in scheme names (e.g., allow "HTTP" as well as "http") for
   125→  // the sake of robustness but should only produce lowercase scheme names for consistency.
   126→  //
   127→  // The validation mode controls whether uppercase letters are permitted.
   128→  absl::string_view scheme = value.getStringView();
   129→
   130→  if (!absl::EqualsIgnoreCase(scheme, "http") && !absl::EqualsIgnoreCase(scheme, "https")) {
   131→    // TODO(#23313) - Honor config setting for mixed case.
   132→    return {HeaderValueValidationResult::Action::Reject,
   133→            UhvResponseCodeDetail::get().InvalidScheme};
   134→  }
   135→
   136→  return HeaderValueValidationResult::success();

    13→// Header value character table.
    14→// From RFC 9110, https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc9110.html#section-5.5:
    15→//
    16→// SPELLCHECKER(off)
    17→// header-field   = field-name ":" OWS field-value OWS
    18→// field-value    = *field-content
    19→// field-content  = field-vchar
    20→//                  [ 1*( SP / HTAB / field-vchar ) field-vchar ]
    21→// field-vchar    = VCHAR / obs-text
    22→// obs-text       = %x80-FF
    23→//
    24→// VCHAR          =  %x21-7E
    25→//                   ; visible (printing) characters
    26→// SPELLCHECKER(on)
    27→inline constexpr std::array<uint32_t, 8> kGenericHeaderValueCharTable = {
    28→    // control characters
    29→    0b00000000010000000000000000000000,
    30→    // !"#$%&'()*+,-./0123456789:;<=>?
    31→    0b11111111111111111111111111111111,
    32→    //@ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ[\]^_
    33→    0b11111111111111111111111111111111,
    34→    //`abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz{|}~
    35→    0b11111111111111111111111111111110,
    36→    // extended ascii
    37→    0b11111111111111111111111111111111,
    38→    0b11111111111111111111111111111111,
    39→    0b11111111111111111111111111111111,
    40→    0b11111111111111111111111111111111,
    41→};
    42→
    43→// :method header character table.
    44→// From RFC 9110: https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc9110.html#section-9.1
    45→//
    46→// SPELLCHECKER(off)
    47→// method = token
    48→// token  = 1*tchar
    49→// tchar  = "!" / "#" / "$" /
... (truncated)

     1→#pragma once
     2→
     3→#include <cstdint>
     4→
     5→#include "source/common/http/character_set_validation.h"
     6→
     7→namespace Envoy {
     8→namespace Extensions {
     9→namespace Http {
    10→namespace HeaderValidators {
    11→namespace EnvoyDefault {
    12→
    13→// Header value character table.
    14→// From RFC 9110, https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc9110.html#section-5.5:
    15→//
    16→// SPELLCHECKER(off)
    17→// header-field   = field-name ":" OWS field-value OWS

Perfect! I've completed a comprehensive analysis of the Envoy v1.31.2 codebase and created the answer file at `/workspace/answer.json`.

## Summary

I found and documented all C++ source files in envoyproxy/envoy that handle HTTP request header injection validation and prevention. The answer includes:

### **Key Findings:**

1. **Header Validator Framework** (`source/extensions/http/header_validators/envoy_default/`):
   - Core validation logic with functions like `validateGenericHeaderName()` and `validateGenericHeaderValue()` that check header characters against RFC-compliant character tables
   - Protocol-specific validators for HTTP/1, HTTP/2
   - All validation is based on **character tables that explicitly exclude CR/LF** characters, preventing CRLF header injection attacks

2. **Character Validation Tables**:
   - `kGenericHeaderValueCharTable`: Allows only visible ASCII and extended ASCII, excluding control characters (CR, LF, NULL)
   - `kGenericHeaderNameCharTable`: RFC 9110 token definition
   - `kPathHeaderCharTable`: RFC 3986 compliant path characters
   - `kMethodHeaderCharTable`: RFC 9110 tchar set

3. **Internal Header Stripping** (`conn_manager_utility.cc`):
   - `cleanInternalHeaders()` function removes internal Envoy headers (x-envoy-*) from edge requests to prevent client injection
   - Strips headers like `x-envoy-retry-on`, `x-envoy-max-retries`, `x-envoy-force-trace`, etc.

4. **Additional Sanitization**:
   - Path normalization with fragment stripping
   - Host header validation with userinfo detection
   - Underscore handling in header names
   - Content-Length and Transfer-Encoding validation
